***забыть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>забыть</a> (338)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zaby̋ti</i>, the composite of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">забути</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zabuty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>забы́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забывать.html>забыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to forget</li>
<li>to neglect</li>
<li>to leave, to forget to bring, to forget to take</li>
<li>to let it go, to let it slip</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запамятовать.html>запа́мятовать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zapámjatovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забыться.html>забы́ться</a> (6148)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>забы́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zabýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забыться.html>забы́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabýtʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забываться.html>забыва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to doze, to drop off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лёг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забыться.html>забы́лся</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On ljóg i <b>zabýlsja</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He lay down and dropped off.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become oblivious, to lose contact with reality
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хо́чет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забыться.html>забы́ться</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On xóčet <b>zabýtʹsja</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He is seeking <b>oblivion</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to forget oneself, to cross the line of what is allowed or to lose control over oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молодой.html>молодо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забываться.html>забыва́йтесь</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ма</a>!</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">imperfective</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Molodój čelovék, ne <b>zabyvájtesʹ</b>, vy ne dóma!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Young man, don't <b>forget yourself</b>, you are not at home!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>забы́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zabýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забываться.html>забыва́ются</a></b>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">imperfective</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nóvyje slová býstro <b>zabyvájutsja</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">New words <b>are/get forgotten</b> quickly.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***завал.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завал.html>зава́л</a> (7717)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завал.html>зава́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завал.html>зава́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завал.html>зава́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завал.html>зава́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>obstruction, blockage, abatis</li>
<li>steep slope</li>
<li>backlog (an accumulation of unfinished work)</li></ol>

***заваливать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заваливать.html>зава́ливать</a> (21005)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завалить.html>завали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заваливать.html>зава́ливать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaválivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завалить.html>завали́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heap up, to bury</li>
<li>to block, to obstruct</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заваливаться.html>зава́ливаться</a> (17776)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заваливать.html>зава́ливать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaválivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заваливаться.html>зава́ливаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaválivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завалиться.html>завали́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lie down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заваливаться.html>зава́ливаться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спать</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaválivatʹsja</b> spatʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall/tumble into bed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tumble down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blow <i>(into)</i>, to blow in, to stroll <i>(into)</i>, to stroll in; to dive <i>(into)</i>, to dive in</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fail, to flop</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заваливать.html>зава́ливать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaválivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завалить.html>завали́ть</a> (3662)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">valítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завалить.html>завали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заваливать.html>зава́ливать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heap up, to bury</li>
<li>to block, to obstruct</li></ol>

***завалиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завалиться.html>завали́ться</a> (7968)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завалить.html>завали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завалиться.html>завали́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavalítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заваливаться.html>зава́ливаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́га</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:завалиться.html>завали́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:диван.html>дива́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kníga <b>zavalílasʹ</b> za diván</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the book has fallen/dropped/slipped behind the sofa</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lie down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завалиться.html>завали́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спать</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavalítʹsja</b> spatʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall/tumble into bed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tumble down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blow <i>(into)</i>, to blow in, to stroll <i>(into)</i>, to stroll in; to dive <i>(into)</i>, to dive in</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fail, to flop
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завалиться.html>завали́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мене</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavalítʹsja</b> na ekzámene</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fail/flunk an exam</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завалить.html>завали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>:
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завалиться.html>завали́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a>; (<a href = vnd.unilang:хоть.html>хоть</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:завалиться.html>завали́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavalítʹsja</b> móžno; (xotʹ) <b>zavalísʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">heaps (of); piles (of)</span></div></dd>

***заваренный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заваренный.html>зава́ренный</a> (10320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***заваривать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заваривать.html>зава́ривать</a> (19194)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заварить.html>завари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavarítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заваривать.html>зава́ривать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavárivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заварить.html>завари́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to brew, to infuse, to steep, <i>(tee, coffee etc)</i> to make</li>
<li>to pour boiling water <i>(over)</i>, to scald</li>
<li>to weld up, to close <i>(up)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заваривать.html>зава́ривать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:каша.html>ка́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavárivatʹ</b> kášu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stir up trouble; make a mess</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***заварить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заварить.html>завари́ть</a> (10320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варить.html>вари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заварить.html>завари́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavarítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заваривать.html>зава́ривать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to brew, to infuse, to steep, <i>(tea, coffee etc)</i> to make</li>
<li>to pour boiling water <i>(over)</i>, to scald</li>
<li>to weld up, to close <i>(up)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заварить.html>завари́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:каша.html>ка́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavarítʹ</b> kášu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stir up trouble; make a mess</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заварить.html>завари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavarítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заварка.html>зава́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavárka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заварка.html>зава́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заварка.html>зава́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заварка.html>зава́рок</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заведовать.html>заве́довать</a> (12825)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заведовать.html>заве́довать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavédovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be in charge, to be the head/chief, to head, to manage</li>
<li>to operate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in terms of factory or office-based environment</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заведующий.html>заве́дующий</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zavédujuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зав.html>зав</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zav</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заведомый.html>заве́домый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavédomyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заведомо.html>заве́домо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavédomo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>deliberately, intentionally, knowingly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:заведомо.html>заве́домо</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:ложный.html>ло́жные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:показание.html>показа́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">davátʹ zavédomo lóžnyje pokazánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deliberately give false witness, to perjure oneself</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>obviously</li></ol>

***заведомый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заведомый.html>заве́домый</a> (24808)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>ве́домый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">védomyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заведомый.html>заве́домый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavédomyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>obvious, notorious

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завезти.html>завезти́</a> (11780)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">veztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завезти.html>завезти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaveztí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завозить.html>завози́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take <i>(to a place)</i>, to drop off <i>(at a place)</i></li>
<li>to supply, to deliver</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заверение.html>завере́ние</a> (17860)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заверить.html>заве́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavéritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
